
ase_stockpile_country_change_direction_to_both_aeroplanes = {
    scope = country

    effect = {
        ase_stockpile_country_change_direction_specific_to_both = {
            goods = aeroplanes
        }
    }

    is_shown = {
        ase_stockpile_country_change_direction_specific_to_both_is_shown = {
            goods = aeroplanes
        }
    }

    is_valid = {
        always = yes
    }

    ai_is_valid = {
        always = no
    }
}
